\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ranking_8py_source_l00934}00934\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ true\ positives\ and\ \`{}\`{}fp\`{}\`{}\ the\ number\ of\ false\ positives.\ The\ precision\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ranking_8py_source_l00935}00935\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ intuitively\ the\ ability\ of\ the\ classifier\ not\ to\ label\ as\ positive\ a\ sample}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ranking_8py_source_l00939}00939\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ true\ positives\ and\ \`{}\`{}fn\`{}\`{}\ the\ number\ of\ false\ negatives.\ The\ recall\ is}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ranking_8py_source_l01535}01535\ \ \ \ \ discount\ =\ 1\ /\ (np.log(np.arange(y\_true.shape[1])\ +\ 2)\ /\ np.log(log\_base))}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ranking_8py_source_l01557}01557\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ induced\ by\ \`{}y\_score\`{})\ is\ replaced\ by\ the\ average\ gain\ within\ this\ group.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ranking_8py_source_l01558}01558\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ discounted\ gain\ for\ a\ tied\ group\ is\ then\ the\ average\ \`{}y\_true\`{}\ within}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ranking_8py_source_l01559}01559\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ this\ group\ times\ the\ sum\ of\ discounts\ of\ the\ corresponding\ ranks.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ranking_8py_source_l01561}01561\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ This\ amounts\ to\ averaging\ scores\ for\ all\ possible\ orderings\ of\ the\ tied}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ranking_8py_source_l01563}01563\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
